<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:допытываться.html>допы́тываться</a> (11274)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">допыта́ться</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dopytátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:допытываться.html>допы́тываться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dopýtyvatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">допыта́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to try to find out, to keep asking <i>(about)</i>, to try to elicit
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:допытываться.html>допы́тывается</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:где.html>где</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>dopýtyvajetsja</b> u menjá, gde vy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he keeps asking me where you are; he is trying to elicit your whereabouts from me</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<li>to finish off, to complete
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:доработать.html>дорабо́тать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:план.html>план</a> [[[СоглашениеRussian|[<a href = vnd.unilang:соглашение.html>соглаше́ние</a>]]]</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dorabótatʹ</b> plan [soglašénije]</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to finalize the plan [agreement]</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to improve, to work further <i>(on)</i></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорасти.html>дорасти́</a> (20988)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>до-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">do-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расти.html>расти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rastí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дорасти.html>дорасти́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dorastí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">дораста́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to grow <i>(to; as high as)</i>, to reach</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be old enough <i>(for; + to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дорасти.html>дорасти́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>dorastí</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">not to be old enough; be too young</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дорасти.html>доро́с</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>того́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:чтобы.html>что́бы</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:пить.html>пить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вино.html>вино́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on ješčó ne <b>dorós</b> (do tovó, štóby) pitʹ vinó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is too young to drink wine</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to rise <i>(to)</i>, to attain the level <i>(of)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дорасти.html>дорасти́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слава.html>сла́вы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dorastí</b> do slávy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to rise to fame</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дорасти.html>доро́с</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:понимание.html>понима́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:писатель.html>писа́теля</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on ne <b>dorós</b> do ponimánija étovo pisátelja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he has a long way to go before he begins to understand this writer</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нос.html>нос</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дорасти.html>доро́с</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nos ne <b>dorós</b> u kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">smb is still wet behind his ears</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">дорва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dorvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дорваться.html>дорва́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dorvátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">дорыва́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pounce on, to fall greedily on, to throw oneself at <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">food, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">do</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cause oneself trouble through frivolous behavior</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to walk up to in rags <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">do</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">дорва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dorvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>до-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">do-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Revolution</i> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дореволюционный.html>дореволюцио́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dorevoljuciónnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>prerevolutionary</li>

***дорога.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>дорога</a> (212)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dorga</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́га</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">doróga</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́ги</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́ги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́г</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>road, way
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>больша́я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́га</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bolʹšája <b>doróga</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">highroad</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:железный.html>желе́зная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́га</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">želéznaja doróga</i> ― <span class="e-translation">railroad (railway)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>passage</li>
<li>trip, journey</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>путь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">putʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стезя.html>стезя́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stezjá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шоссе.html>шоссе́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">šossɛ́</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трасса.html>тра́сса</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">trássa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">автотра́сса</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">avtotrássa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дороговизна.html>дорогови́зна</a> (23637)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>дорого́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dorogój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-изна</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-izna</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дороговизна.html>дорогови́зна</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dorogovízna</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дороговизна.html>дорогови́зны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дороговизна.html>дорогови́зны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дороговизна.html>дорогови́зн</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dearness (being expensive)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Often stressed as <i><a href = vnd.unilang:дороговизна.html>дороговизна́</a></i>, which is not recognized by dictionaries.</li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ро<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>го<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:виза.html>ви́з</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. </p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-дорог-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-ов-изн</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

***дорогой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>дорогой</a> (1396)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dorgъ</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:драга.html>драго́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dragój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a borrowing from Old Church Slavonic.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>дорого́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dorogój</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)доро́же</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">дорожа́йший</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dear</li>
<li>expensive</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>In the sense of "my dear", this word is not restricted to use between men and women, but is quite common between friends of the same sex, or a teacher to any of his students without regard to sex. When used between men, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мой</a> <a class="mw-selflink selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>дорогой</a></a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">moj dorogoj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> usually is not translated, since English does not possess a good unisex counterpart to this.</li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дорогой.html>до́рого</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dórogo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дороговизна.html>дорогови́зна</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dorogovízna</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дорогуша.html>дорогу́ша</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dorogúša</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дорожать.html>дорожа́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dorožátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">подорожа́ние</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podorožánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дорогостоящий.html>дорогосто́ящий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dorogostójaščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***дородный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дородный.html>доро́дный</a> (11210)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">дородьныи</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dorodĭnyi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dorodьnъ</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">дорі́дний</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dorídnyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">productive; tall, large; natural, innate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">dorodny</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">healthy; beautiful; mature</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Meanings such as "healthy", "beautiful", "good", "productive", etc. can be found dialectally in Russian. Per ESSJa, from Proto-Slavic <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*do-</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*rodъ</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ьnъ</i>; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>до-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">do-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rod</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дородный.html>доро́дный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">doródnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)доро́днее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)доро́дней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>plump, chubby, corpulent</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рослый.html>ро́слый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">róslyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полный.html>по́лный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pólnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***дорожавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорожавший.html>дорожа́вший</a> (29703)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дорожавший.html>дорожа́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dorožávšij</span>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>дорого́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dorogój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дорожить.html>дорожи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dorožítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to value, to prize
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дорожить.html>дорожи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́менем</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dorožítʹ</b> svoím vrémenem</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to value one's time</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to take care of, to value
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дорожить.html>дорожи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:добрый.html>до́брым</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:имя.html>и́менем</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dorožítʹ</b> svoím dóbrym ímenem</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to value one's good name</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to not to waste, to use wisely</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>досада</a> (4129)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dosada</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>annoyance, nuisance, vexation</li>
<li>disappointment</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:досадный.html>доса́дный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dosádnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:досадный.html>доса́дно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dosádno</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-доса́дно" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)доса́днее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-доса́дно" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)доса́дней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>annoyingly, distressingly
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:досадный.html>доса́дно</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сознательный.html>созна́тельный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>своего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бессилие.html>бесси́лия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dosádno</b> soznátelʹnyj svojevó bessílija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">distressingly conscious of one's powerlessness</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>доса́да</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dosáda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:досадный.html>доса́дный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dosádnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)доса́днее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)доса́дней</b>)

<ol><li>annoying, vexatious, disappointing, deplorable, regrettable, troublesome
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:досадный.html>доса́дная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ошибка.html>оши́бка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dosádnaja</b> ošíbka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">annoying/regrettable mistake</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>distressed, vexed <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">expressing distress or vexation</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of tears, a look, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:досадный.html>доса́дный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:взгляд.html>взгляд</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dosádnyj</b> vzgljad</i> ― <span class="e-translation">distressed look</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***доска.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:доска.html>доска́</a> (1320)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dъska</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*diskuz</i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">discus</i>. See there for details.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доска.html>доска́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">doská</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доска.html>доски́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доска.html>до́ски</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доска.html>досо́к</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доска.html>до́сок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>board, plank
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лыжа.html>лы́жи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:доска.html>доски́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">lýži iz <b>doskí</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">skis made from boards</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>blackboard
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:классный.html>кла́ссная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:доска.html>доска́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">klássnaja doská</i> ― <span class="e-translation">blackboard</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>plate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">гри́фельная <b><a href = vnd.unilang:доска.html>доска́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">grífelʹnaja <b>doská</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">slate</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:доска.html>доски́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:доска.html>доски́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ot <b>doskí</b> do <b>doskí</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">from cover to cover</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дос.html>дос</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка́</b>
